 Promise Day 2019: aaj promis de he
 Usually, on Promise Day, people promise to live with their partners for life
 lekin is promis de aap partner ke saath khud se healdi lifestil or diet follow karne kaa promis bhi jarur karen, kyonki har vyakti ke liye acchhee sehat bahut myne rakhti he
 If you remain healthy, then you will be able to keep your partner happy too and will be able to fulfill their needs
 1
 Stay away from junk food - In modern life people consume more junk food
 lekin aapaki ye aadat aapaki sehat ko nuksaan pahunchaa sakati he
 Therefore, Promise yourself to minimize your intake of junk food this Promise Day
 2
 Make Routines - Set a time for your food and drinks
 samay ke anusaar khaanaa khaaen
 This will not only improve your eating habits, but will also benefit your health
 3
 Exercise - To stay healthy, exercising with healthy food is also very important
 eksrasij ko apni rojaanaa kii routine kaa hissaa bana len
 Do walk after eating food
 4
 Drink water without being thirsty - do not wait to get thirsty to drink water
 dinabhar main kam se kam 8 gilaas pani jarur pien
 If you are not able to drink that much water, then you can drink lemon juice mixed with water
 isse aap hydrateed rahenge or vajan bhi control main rahegaa
 5
 rojaanaa fal or subjiyon kaa seven karen-apni diet main taaji subjiyon or falon kaa seven jarur karen
 Nutrients present in these keep you healthy and also protect you from many diseases
 aapako jaanakar hairaani hogi ki subjiyon or falon ke seven se kabj, dil kii beemaari ke saath cancer hone kaa khatra bhi kam hota he
 Therefore, do the Promise to stay healthy by yourself this Promise Day
